Cute little hole in the wall that serves savory and sweet crepes, coffee and a few other odds and ends. The crepes are pretty good and include inventive combinations of veggies, cheese and meats. < Review>
Was there recently on Sunday at around 12:30, perhaps their busiest time of the week.  I ordered an Oslo crepe that was supposed to have smoked salmon, cream cheese, tomatoes and capers.  After waiting what seemed like a long time, I received my order.  I'll give them a pass on the time because there were 2 guys making crepes as fast as they could on a busy Sunday brunch rush, but I won't excuse the fact that there were no capers in my crepe.  If they had run out, someone should have let me know.  It may be that they were just forgotten.  I don't know.  But it was advertised so there's no good excuse.<//Review>

I've patronized this business for eight years. In the early morning hours of March 30, 2018, I stopped by to purchase gasoline. When I attempted to use the men's bathroom, it was locked. Couldn't understand why it was locked when I was the only patronized on the premises.

I will buy my gasoline from another location from now on.< /Text>

< Review>
This place is a little smaller than some of the other big chain clubs, but the prices are a lot better, and they still have all the equipment you could want. This location in particular is a lot busier after work hours than other place, but I'm still able to get a full workout in (warm up, weight training, and 30 minutes of cardio) in an hour and a half.

Facilities are pretty nice and new, but they do have some problems in the men's bathroom with the toilets leaking on the floor. Also, when things go down, they don't get fixed very quickly. I've been going here for a couple of months now, and the water bottle refill station that said it was out if order when I started is still out of order, and the shower stall in the men's that was down took like a month to fix.

Overall, it's a nice gym for price. They have a few extra things like tanning and hydro massage, and some 3D fitness modeler that I'm not sure exactly what it does (maybe shows you what you look like in better shape?). They have group classes and personal training just like every other gym. I'd say if they fixed things at a more reasonable rate it would be 5 star.< /Review>

<text>I cannot speak highly enough of Trojan Athletics. I have been working out here for almost a year and can attest to its strengths: knowledgeable coaches, clean facility, and great community.

Coaching ‚Äî The coaches at Trojan are incredibly attentive and extremely knowledgeable about CrossFit and weightlifting. I came to Trojan as a complete beginner; I had never used a barbell or done any kind of Metcon training. What I noticed immediately is that ALL the coaches took the time to train me properly and ensure that I was completing movements correctly. Crossfit sometimes gets a bad name due to athlete injuries, but the coaches at Trojan truly invest in helping beginner athletes form correct habits and advanced athletes modify their technique.

Classes ‚Äî Classes are offered throughout the day and up until 8 pm, which was a huge bonus for people (like myself) who work late. The classes are TOUGH and will push an athlete both mentally and physically to achieve his or her fitness goals. After a short time training here, I began to notice changes in my strength, body composition, and muscle mass.

Community ‚Äî The people who train at Trojan are a close knit community. The athletes here are a diverse group of ALL skill levels and are extremely welcoming. During the CrossFit open, the sense of camaraderie was exceptional. We all stayed to watch our friends in hourly heats. Memorial Day and Regionals offer other opportunities to compete and have fun.

I highly recommend Trojan Athletics to athletes of any skill level or desired fitness goals.< /text>< pictures>

< Review>
Nice people workout here. Weightlifting and crossfit equipments are plenty and facility conditions are ok. But read your contracts carefully and treat every transaction like a serious business dealing regardless of how much time you spent here. Being meek, agreeable, or expecting personalized services can (repeatedly) incur financial consequences.

Edit after reply: I do not mean to object to any contracts I signed up. Other gyms employ such policies. However, as an old member staying for years through a few ups and downs of this place, I do feel entitled to a bit more friendly reminders on changes of terms when they applies to me (i.e. I do not recall any mention of the cancellation policies except buried inside the contract, which of course I should've read, when I asked to change my plans). Similar misunderstandings had happened before, and those times I backed down (as is this time except this feedback) because the specific situations were reasonable from the gym's perspective. However, such occurrences without much leeway do not make me feel like a valued member of the community.

(besides, shouldn't the proper *business* response to a request of cancellation at a date specifically showing my ignorance of the policy be "That cannot be done because your contract would not allow it. Earliest possible date is ..." instead of "Confirmed!" ?)<//Review>

< Text>
I have been coming here for quite a few years and i don't think I've ever had something that wasn't delicious. The service over the years has been hit & miss but this time our waitress was attentive and our order came out surprisingly quick. Of course we left fat & bloated LOL! If you like eggs benedict, they have one of the largest selections of different types to choose from. If you are seated on the left side near the large mural, while you are waiting for your food, check out all the "little surprises" and secret little items or characters randomly scattered into the landscape. Someone had some fun with that and we seem to find something each time that we hadn't seen before. They are super busy during your typical brunch hours so we prefer to go a little closer to lunchtime if its a weekend. Weekdays don't seem to be as bad.</Text>
